### [1] [Temporal Contrastive Transformer for Financial Crime Detection: Self-Supervised Sequence Embeddings via Predictive Contrastive Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21490)
*Danny Butvinik,Yonit Marcus,Nitzan Tal,Gabrielle Azoulay*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出时间对比变换器（TCT），一种自监督对比学习框架，用于对金融交易序列进行行为表征学习。实验表明其嵌入特征单独使用时达到AUC 0.8644，但与领域工程特征结合时无显著提升（AUC 0.9205 vs 0.9245），表明学习到的表征与现有特征抽象高度重叠。尽管尚未达到生产就绪水平，但该方法展示了减少对人工特征工程依赖的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有金融欺诈检测高度依赖人工设计的领域特征工程，开发成本高且难以捕捉时间序列中的上下文动态。作者希望提出一种自监督表征学习方法，自动从金融交易序列中学习行为时间模式，以减轻对人工特征工程的依赖。

Method: 提出TCT（Temporal Contrastive Transformer）框架，采用自监督对比学习目标训练Transformer模型，对金融交易序列进行上下文时间动态表征学习。下游任务使用梯度提升分类器（如XGBoost）评估嵌入特征效果。

Result: 单独使用TCT嵌入特征：AUC 0.8644，表明模型捕获了有意义的时序结构；TCT嵌入+工程特征组合：AUC 0.9205 vs 仅工程特征基线：AUC 0.9245，两者无显著差异，说明学习表征与现有特征抽象高度重叠。

Conclusion: TCT作为表征学习方法能有效捕获相关行为信号，但当前阶段在强领域特征基础上难以实现额外增益。达到与强工程基线相当的性能本身是有意义的成果，表明学习表征能在无人工工程条件下逼近领域特定特征，为减少金融欺诈检测中对特征工程的依赖提供了有希望的方向。

Abstract: We introduce the Temporal Contrastive Transformer (TCT), a representation learning framework designed to capture contextual temporal dynamics in sequences of financial transactions. The model is trained using a self-supervised contrastive objective to produce embeddings that encode behavioral patterns over time, with the goal of supporting downstream fraud detection tasks. We evaluate TCT in a realistic setting by using the learned embeddings as input features to a gradient boosting classifier. Experimental results show that embeddings alone achieve meaningful predictive performance (AUC 0.8644), indicating that the model captures non-trivial temporal structure. However, when combined with domain-engineered features, no measurable improvement is observed over the baseline (AUC 0.9205 vs. 0.9245), suggesting that the learned representations largely overlap with existing feature abstractions. These findings position TCT as a promising representation learning approach that captures relevant behavioral signal, while highlighting the challenges of achieving additive value over strong domain features. The results reflect an intermediate stage in the development of temporal representation learning for financial crime detection and motivate further research on model architecture, training objectives, and integration strategies. At this early stage, achieving performance comparable to a strong feature-engineered baseline is itself a meaningful outcome, indicating that learned representations approximate domain-specific features without manual engineering. While not yet production-ready, these results point to a promising direction for reducing reliance on feature engineering in financial crime detection.

</details>


### [2] [Teaching Language Models to Forecast Research Success Through Comparative Idea Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21491)
*Srujan P Mule,Aniketh Garikaparthi,Manasi Patwardhan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究语言模型能否在不进行实验的情况下预测研究想法的实证成功。通过构建包含11,488个想法对的数据集，发现SFT训练的小模型（77.1%准确率）优于GPT-5（61.1%），而RLVR方法可在提供可解释理由的同时达到71.35%准确率，展示了计算高效的小语言模型作为客观验证器的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着语言模型加速科学研究，评估和筛选大量AI生成的研究想法成为新的瓶颈。本文旨在探索能否让语言模型在无需详尽实验的情况下，预测研究想法的实证成功，从而为自主科学发现提供可扩展的验证路径。

Method: 论文研究比较性实证预测：给定基准测试目标和两个候选想法，预测哪个表现更好。构建了基于PapersWithCode客观结果的11,488个想法对数据集。采用SFT和RLVR（基于可验证奖励的强化学习）两种训练方法，将评估建模为推理任务，训练模型发现潜在推理路径。

Result: 现成8B参数模型仅30%准确率；SFT训练后达到77.1%，超过GPT-5的61.1%；RLVR方法达到71.35%且提供可解释理由。通过消融实验和分布外测试，证明模型对表面启发式具有鲁棒性，并能迁移到跨领域时间分割测试集和独立构建的测试集。

Conclusion: 计算高效的小语言模型可以作为有效的客观验证器，为自主科学发现提供可扩展的路径。

Abstract: As language models accelerate scientific research by automating hypothesis generation and implementation, a new bottleneck emerges: evaluating and filtering hundreds of AI-generated ideas without exhaustive experimentation. We ask whether LMs can learn to forecast the empirical success of research ideas before any experiments are run. We study comparative empirical forecasting: given a benchmark-specific research goal and two candidate ideas, predict which will achieve better benchmark performance. We construct a dataset of 11,488 idea pairs grounded in objective outcomes from PapersWithCode. While off-the-shelf 8B-parameter models struggle (30% acc.), SFT dramatically boosts performance to 77.1%, outperforming GPT-5 (61.1%). By framing evaluation as a reasoning task via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), we train models to discover latent reasoning paths, achieving 71.35% acc. with interpretable justifications. Through additional ablations and out-of-distribution tests, we show robustness to surface-level heuristics and transfer to both a cross-domain time-split test set and an independently constructed test set. Our results demonstrate that compute-efficient small language models can serve as effective, objective verifiers, offering a scalable path for autonomous scientific discovery.

</details>


### [3] [SepsisAI Orchestrator: A Containerized and Scalable Platform for Deploying AI Models and Real-Time Monitoring in Early Sepsis Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22331)
*Santiago Ospitia,John Sanabria,John Garcia-Henao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了SepsisAI-Orchestrator，一个开源模块化平台，用于解决早期败血症检测模型从研究到临床部署的工程障碍。平台集成了FHIR-inspired CDA预处理、NoSQL存储、容器化LightGBM分类器（REST API）和Streamlit仪表盘，通过Docker/Kubernetes编排。在12线程CPU上复制数从3扩至12时，p95延迟降低57.3%（从3.3s降至1.41s）并消除请求失败，而过量扩至24/48副本因调度争用导致性能下降，揭示了临床AI推理负载中U型扩展曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床机器学习模型虽预测性能优异，但受限于异构数据表示、缺乏标准化部署流程以及研究原型与医院环境并发/延迟要求不匹配等系统级障碍，模型向床边转化受限。作者旨在通过构建一个集成平台来弥合这一部署鸿沟。

Method: 构建SepsisAI-Orchestrator平台：采用HL7 FHIR启发式CDA进行数据预处理，NoSQL存储，容器化LightGBM分类器通过REST API提供服务，Streamlit构建临床仪表盘，全部通过Docker和Kubernetes编排。使用k6工具在50-1000并发虚拟用户下进行负载测试，系统性地改变副本数（3, 6, 12, 24, 48）以评估扩展性能。

Result: 在12线程CPU上，副本数从3扩至12时，p95延迟从3.3s降至1.41s（降低57.3%），请求失败完全消除；但继续扩至24或48副本时，由于调度器争用导致性能下降。这种U型扩展行为在临床AI推理负载中此前未被量化。

Conclusion: SepsisAI-Orchestrator证明了通过合理的工程基础设施可以有效解决临床AI模型部署瓶颈。关键的实践发现是副本数必须与宿主物理CPU线程数匹配，过量副本不仅无益反而有害。平台开源于GitHub，但未进行前瞻性临床验证。

Abstract: Despite strong predictive results in the clinical machine learning literature, the translation of these models into bedside use remains limited by systems-level barriers: heterogeneous data representations, the absence of standardized deployment workflows, and a mismatch between research prototypes and the concurrency and latency requirements of hospital environments. We present the SepsisAI-Orchestrator, an open-source modular platform that addresses this deployment gap for early sepsis detection. The platform integrates HL7 FHIR-inspired Clinical Document Architecture (CDA) preprocessing, NoSQL storage, a containerized LightGBM classifier served via REST APIs, and a Streamlit clinical dashboard, orchestrated with Docker and Kubernetes. A previously validated LightGBM model (F1 0.87-0.94 on PhysioNet 2019) is reused without modification; the contribution lies in the surrounding infrastructure and its empirical characterization under load. Using k6 with 50-1000 concurrent virtual users, we find that replica count must be matched to the physical CPU thread count of the host: scaling from 3 to 12 replicas on a 12-thread CPU reduces p95 latency from 3.3s to 1.41s (57.3% reduction) and eliminates all request failures, while over-provisioning to 24 or 48 replicas degrades performance due to scheduler contention. To our knowledge this U-shaped scaling behavior has not been quantified previously for clinical AI inference workloads. We do not claim prospective clinical validation. Source code and deployment manifests are available at https://github.com/nucleusai/sepsisai-orchestrator.

</details>


### [4] [Double descent for least-squares interpolation on contaminated data: A simulation study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21494)
*Tino Werner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了过参数化线性回归模型中，当训练数据被污染（存在异常值）时，是否会出现"双重下降"现象。结果表明，高度非鲁棒的最小二乘插值估计器在高度过参数化下确实展现出双重下降，其泛化性能甚至优于鲁棒替代方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在数据被污染（存在异常值）的线性回归环境中，过参数化模型是否仍能表现出双重下降现象，并比较鲁棒与非鲁棒估计器在此场景下的泛化性能。

Method: 在含污染数据的线性回归框架下，对比高度非鲁棒的最小二乘插值估计器与多种鲁棒替代方法的泛化性能，分析模型复杂度与泛化误差之间的关系。

Result: 高度过参数化下，最小二乘插值估计器展现出双重下降现象，其泛化性能甚至超过鲁棒替代方法。

Conclusion: 过参数化不仅能在干净数据下改善泛化，在数据被污染的情况下也能使非鲁棒估计器获得优于鲁棒方法的泛化性能，这挑战了传统鲁棒统计的直觉。

Abstract: Overparametrized models can exhibit an excellent generalization performance, although they should be prone to overfitting according to classical statistical theory. The discovery of the "double descent", indicating that the generalization error decreases after a certain model complexity has been reached, opened a new line of research. Robust statistics considers statistical estimation on contaminated data, which, due to assumptions that do not hold on real data, let data points appear as outliers w.r.t. the assumed "ideal" distribution, potentially severely distorting any classical estimator. We address the question whether a double descent phenomenon can be observed in a linear regression setting with contaminated training data. We compare the performance of the highly non-robust least-squares interpolation estimator with several robust alternatives. It turns out that large overparametrization indeed allows for a double descent phenomenon, resulting in a very good generalization performance of the least-squares interpolator, surpassing that of the robust alternatives.

</details>


### [5] [HealthCraft: A Reinforcement Learning Safety Environment for Emergency Medicine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21496)
*Brandon Dent*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HealthCraft是基于Corecraft改编的首个公开强化学习环境，用于在真实急诊医学条件下评估轨迹级安全性。它包含FHIR R4世界状态（14种实体类型、3,987个种子实体）、24个MCP工具、双层评分规则（安全关键标准违规即零奖励），以及195个任务（2,255个二元标准，其中515个安全关键）。在Claude Opus 4.6和GPT-5.4上的评估显示，Pass@1分别为24.8%和12.6%，安全失败率27.5%和34.0%；多步工作流性能接近零（1.0%和0.0%）。基础设施bug修复会改变模型排名，验证了基础设施保真度是评估的一部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿语言模型正被部署到临床工作流中，但缺乏安全评估基础设施。静态医疗QA基准无法捕捉急诊医学中的关键失败模式：轨迹级安全崩溃、工具误用以及在持续临床压力下的妥协。

Method: 基于Corecraft构建HealthCraft环境，采用FHIR R4世界状态、24个MCP工具、双层评分规则（安全违规零奖励），定义195个任务（2,255个二元标准），使用确定性LLM评判器覆盖降低评估噪声，并设计了60次负类烟测试验证奖励信号不可直接用于训练。

Result: V8评估：Claude Opus 4.6 Pass@1为24.8%[21.5-28.4]，安全失败率27.5%；GPT-5.4 Pass@1为12.6%[10.2-15.6]，安全失败率34.0%。多步工作流性能接近零（Claude 1.0%，GPT-5.4 0.0%）。基础设施bug修复（v2到v8共6个）会改变模型排名。负类烟测试显示约束标准通过率0.929，存在可被评估容忍但训练奖励不可接受的游戏化风险。

Conclusion: 当前最先进模型在急诊医学轨迹级安全评估中表现极差，多步工作流性能近乎为零。基础设施保真度直接影响评估结果和模型排名。HealthCraft环境、任务、评分规则和评估框架已开源（Apache 2.0），为未来LLM临床安全训练奖励研究提供了基础平台。

Abstract: Frontier language models are being deployed into clinical workflows faster than the infrastructure to evaluate them safely. Static medical-QA benchmarks miss the failure modes that matter in emergency medicine: trajectory-level safety collapse, tool misuse, and capitulation under sustained clinical pressure. We present HealthCraft, the first public reinforcement-learning environment that rewards trajectory-level safety under realistic emergency-medicine conditions, adapted from Corecraft. It is built on a FHIR R4 world state with 14 entity types and 3,987 seed entities, exposes 24 MCP tools, and defines a dual-layer rubric that zeroes reward whenever any safety-critical criterion is violated. We release 195 tasks across six categories, graded against 2,255 binary criteria (515 safety-critical); a post-hoc 10-task negative-class slate extends this to 205 tasks and 2,337 criteria. V8 results on two frontier models show Claude Opus 4.6 at Pass@1 24.8% [21.5-28.4] and GPT-5.4 at 12.6% [10.2-15.6], with safety-failure rates of 27.5% and 34.0%. On multi-step workflows - the closest proxy to real emergency care - performance collapses to near zero (Claude 1.0%, GPT-5.4 0.0%) despite partial competence on individual steps. Six infrastructure bugs fixed between pilots v2 and v8 re-ordered which model "looks stronger," evidence that infrastructure fidelity is part of the measurement. A deterministic LLM-judge overlay bounds evaluator noise, and a 60-run negative-class smoke pilot shows the reward signal is not drop-in training-safe: restraint criteria pass at 0.929 prevalence, a gameability an eval harness can tolerate but a training reward cannot. We scaffold coupling to a Megatron+SGLang+GRPO loop per Corecraft Section 5.2 and leave training-reward ablations as future work. Environment, tasks, rubrics, and harness are released under Apache 2.0.

</details>


### [6] [Harnesses for Inference-Time Alignment over Execution Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21516)
*Boyuan Wang,Bochao Li,Minghan Wang,Yuxin Tao,Fang Kong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从推理时轨迹对齐的角度研究LLM Agent的"缰绳"（Harness）设计，将Harness分解为任务分解和引导执行两个机制，量化了工作流粒度、重试预算和引导动作重新加权对性能的影响，揭示了过度分解、过度剪枝和幻觉执行等失效模式，并发现部分指定初始步骤的Harness可能比完整结构化工作流更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的Harness设计缺乏统一的理论框架来理解其不同设计选择对性能的影响，且存在"更精细的Harness并不一致更好"的现象，需要从理论上阐明何时以及为何某些Harness设计会失效。

Method: 提出推理时轨迹对齐的视角，将Harness分解为任务分解（将任务结构化为子目标）和引导执行（在执行过程中重塑局部动作分布）两个独立机制，并定量分析工作流粒度、重试预算和引导动作重新加权对性能极限的影响。

Result: 识别出过度分解、过度剪枝和幻觉执行三种具体失效模式，并通过受控合成实验和真实终端Agent基准验证了理论预测。发现部分指定初始步骤的Harness（将剩余执行留给Agent）比完整结构化工作流能达到更高的通过率。

Conclusion: 有效的Harness设计不需要完全结构化，部分指定（尤其是初始步骤）的方式在保持引导优势的同时避免了过度约束带来的失效模式，为实际Agent系统设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Harness engineering has emerged as an important inference-time technique for large language model (LLM) agents, aiming to improve long-term performance through task decomposition and guided execution. However, more elaborate harnesses are not uniformly better: increasing decomposition or guidance can sometimes improve execution, but can also reduce final task success. We study harness design through the lens of inference-time trajectory alignment. This perspective separates harness into two mechanisms: task decomposition, which structures a task into sub-goals, and guided execution, which reshapes local action distributions during execution. This decomposition allows us to quantify how workflow granularity, retry budgets, and guidance-induced action reweighting shape the performance limits of harness design. It further reveals concrete failure modes, including over-decomposition, over-pruning, and hallucinated execution. We validate these predictions through controlled synthetic experiments and real terminal agent benchmarks. Inspired by the theory, we further show that effective harnesses can be partial: specifying only the initial steps and leaving the remaining execution to agent can achieve higher pass rate than fully structured workflows.

</details>


### [7] [A Reproducible Log-Driven AutoML Framework for Interpretable Pipeline Optimization in Healthcare Risk Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21528)
*Rui Huang,Lican Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出yvsoucom-iterkit，一个确定性、日志驱动的自动化机器学习框架，将pipeline优化编码为可复现的配置级系统。在糖尿病和中风数据集上评估了18,000+种配置，揭示了搜索空间的结构化冗余性，发现少量关键组件（数据增强、模型选择、不平衡处理）主导性能，并通过集成模型实现了稳定的高F1分数（Weighted-F1: 0.89-0.94）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有疾病风险预测面临特征异质、样本有限和类别不平衡等挑战，且AutoML的可复现性和组件间交互分析不足。

Method: 提出yvsoucom-iterkit确定性自动化机器学习框架，将每个pipeline编码为可追踪的日志实体，支持组件归因、交互、相似性和跨种子鲁棒性分析。使用随机森林重要性分析、RMS距离相似度分析等方法对18,000+配置进行系统评估。

Result: Pima数据集上Weighted-F1达0.89、Macro-F1达0.88；Stroke数据集上Weighted-F1达0.94、Macro-F1为0.67。关键组件重要性：Pima中数据增强0.454、模型选择0.198、不平衡处理0.101；Stroke中不平衡处理0.406。组件相似性分析显示特征选择变体间RMS距离仅0.0252，mixup与无增强相似度0.0279，TomekLinks与无不平衡处理相似度0.0325。集成模型跨种子变异性0.023-0.026，低于SVM。

Conclusion: 有效AutoML优化可聚焦于少量高影响力组件；搜索空间存在结构冗余；集成模型在性能和鲁棒性间取得更好平衡。

Abstract: Accurate and reproducible disease risk prediction remains challenging due to heterogeneous features, limited samples, and severe class imbalance. This study introduces yvsoucom-iterkit, a deterministic and log-driven automated machine learning framework that formulates pipeline optimization as a fully reproducible, configuration-level system. Each pipeline is encoded as a traceable log entity, enabling analysis of component attribution, interactions, similarity, and cross-seed robustness. Experiments on the Pima Indians Diabetes and Stroke datasets across more than 18,000 pipeline configurations reveal a structured and partially redundant search space, where performance is governed by a small subset of interacting components. Random Forest importance analysis identifies augmentation (0.454), model choice (0.198), and imbalance handling (0.101) as key drivers on Pima, while imbalance handling dominates Stroke (0.406). Component similarity analysis shows strong redundancy, with feature selection variants (biMax-biMean) exhibiting low RMS distance (0.0252), mixup closely matching no augmentation (0.0279), and TomekLinks aligning with no imbalance handling (0.0325), whereas Gaussian noise shows greater divergence from no augmentation (0.10). The framework achieves strong and stable performance using ensemble models (Weighted-F1 0.89, Macro-F1 0.88 on Pima; Weighted-F1 0.94 on Stroke), while Macro-F1 remains lower on Stroke (0.67) due to class imbalance. Cross-seed analysis reveals a performance-robustness trade-off, with ensembles showing lower variability (0.023-0.026) than SVM. These results indicate that effective AutoML optimization can focus on a reduced set of high-impact components.

</details>


### [8] [DualOptim+: Bridging Shared and Decoupled Optimizer States for Better Machine Unlearning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21539)
*Xuyang Zhong,Qizhang Li,Yiwen Guo,Chen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出DualOptim+框架，通过基础状态和增量状态架构改进大语言模型机器遗忘，并引入8bit量化变体，在多个任务中实现了更好的目标权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型机器遗忘中，遗忘目标和保留目标之间存在梯度方向冲突，现有方法难以在两者间取得良好平衡。

Method: 引入基础状态（base state）捕获遗忘和保留目标的共享表示，以及增量状态（delta states）保留目标特定残差；优化器根据梯度方向冲突自适应地桥接共享和解耦状态；还提出8bit量化变体降低内存开销。

Result: 在虚构和真实世界遗忘、安全对齐、多任务学习任务中，DualOptim+一致地在不同目标之间实现了更优的权衡。

Conclusion: DualOptim+框架有效提升了LLM机器遗忘的性能，8bit量化版本在不牺牲性能前提下降低内存开销。

Abstract: We propose DualOptim+, a novel optimization framework for improving machine unlearning in large language models. It introduces a base state to capture common representations shared by forgetting and retaining objectives and delta states to preserve objective-specific residuals. This architecture allows the optimizer to adaptively bridge shared and decoupled states based on the directional conflict between forgetting and retaining gradients. We further introduce DualOptim+ 8bit, a quantized variant that reduces memory overhead without compromising performance. Extensive experiments across fictitious and real-world unlearning, safety alignment, and multi-task learning tasks demonstrate that DualOptim+ consistently achieves a superior trade-off between different objectives. Codes are available at https://github.com/CityU-MLO/DualOptimPlus.

</details>


### [9] [Provable Joint Decontamination for Benchmarking Multiple Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21543)
*Zhenlong Liu,Hao Zeng,Hongxin Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出联合包络共形选择（JECS）方法，将多模型基准去污染形式化为联合选择问题，通过共形p值聚合和包络重构实现全局污染率（GCR）的可控选择，实验证明其在保持GCR控制的同时比max-p基线具有更高统计效力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准数据污染检测方法存在两大不足：基于评分的方法缺乏理论保证，而单模型共形方法只能对单个模型进行污染控制，分别应用于多个模型会产生模型特定的基准，无法实现跨模型的公平比较。

Method: JECS包含三个步骤：(1) 计算每模型的共形p值；(2) 按样本取各模型p值的最大值进行聚合；(3) 从右尾观测值中重构max-p在原假设下的保守包络分布，再对包络缩放后的值应用自适应Benjamini-Hochberg过程进行选择，从而在整体上控制全局污染率。

Result: 在多种模型和基准上的广泛实验表明，JECS相比max-p基线具有更高的统计效力（power），且能持续稳定地维持目标全局污染率（GCR）控制。

Conclusion: JECS为多模型基准去污染提供了首个具有GCR理论保证的共形选择框架，有效解决了跨模型公平比较的污染控制问题。

Abstract: Benchmark data contamination has become a central challenge in LLM evaluation: when evaluation examples appear in the training data of one or more audited models, reported performance can be inflated and cross-model comparisons become unreliable. A broad line of training-data detection work designs scores to quantify how strongly a model memorizes a given data point, but these score-based methods lack theoretical guarantees. Recent conformal approaches provide provable false-identification control for a single model; however, applying them separately to each model can produce model-specific benchmarks, undermining fair comparison across models. In this work, we formalize multi-model benchmark decontamination as a joint selection problem and propose Joint Envelope Conformal Selection (JECS), a conformal procedure that enables global contamination rate (GCR) control under stated assumptions. Specifically, JECS computes per-model conformal p-values, aggregates them by the per-item maximum, and reconstructs a conservative envelope of the max-p null distribution from right-tail observations above a data-driven threshold. By applying the adaptive Benjamini-Hochberg (BH) procedure to the envelope-rescaled values, we select a benchmark with provable GCR control. Extensive experiments across various models and benchmarks demonstrate that JECS achieves higher power than the max-p baseline while consistently maintaining the target GCR control.

</details>

However, the practical deployment of NIR sensors still depends on calibration models able to handle high-dimensional, collinear spectra, limited sample sizes, preprocessing dependence, spectral outliers, and extrapolation beyond the calibration domain. Here, we evaluate whether tabular foundation models can provide a new calibration strategy for NIR chemical sensing. We benchmark TabPFN on 66 NIR datasets covering 54 regression and 12 classification tasks, and compare direct inference on raw spectra with preprocessing-optimized inference against PLS/PLS-DA, Ridge, Catboost, and one-dimensional convolutional neural networks. The study uses a unified validation framework in which preprocessing and model selection are performed exclusively on calibration data before external test evaluation. In regression, preprocessing-optimized TabPFN achieves the best overall average rank and significantly outperforms PLS, CatBoost, TabPFN on raw spectra, and CNN-1D, while remaining statistically comparable to Ridge. These results suggest that tabular foundation models can complement established chemometric workflows for NIR chemical sensing, especially in small- to medium-sized calibration settings, while highlighting the need for spectroscopy-specific priors and uncertainty-aware deployment strategies.

### [11] [Expectation Consistency Loss: Rethink Confidence Calibration under Covariate Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21552)
*Jinzong Dong,Zhaohui Jiang,Bo Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于期望一致性条件（Expectation consistency condition）的置信度校准方法（ECL），用于解决协变量偏移下的分类模型校准问题，该方法无需密度比估计，兼容多种校准类型，并在理论和实验上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有置信度校准方法大多假设训练与测试数据独立同分布，在协变量偏移下效果受限；而已有的协变量偏移校准方法存在类级/规范校准困难、依赖不稳定的重要性加权（当密度比过大或无界时）等问题。本文旨在克服这些局限性，重新思考协变量偏移下的置信度校准。

Method: 首先推导出协变量偏移下置信度校准的充要条件——期望一致性条件，揭示协变量偏移不一定导致校准失效；基于该条件提出无监督域适应损失ECL，兼容规范校准、类级校准和顶标签校准；证明ECL的计算复杂度与ECE相同，并提供基于理论的小批量训练方案。

Result: 在模拟和真实协变量偏移数据集上验证了ECL方法的有效性，表明其在协变量偏移下能有效校准模型置信度，且优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 协变量偏移下存在比全局分布对齐更弱的校准条件（期望一致性条件），基于此设计的ECL损失函数能够稳定、高效地实现目标域的置信度校准，为安全关键场景下的模型部署提供了可靠保障。

Abstract: Confidence calibration for classification models is vital in safety-critical decision-making scenarios and has received extensive attention. General confidence calibration methods assume training and test data are independent and identically distributed, limiting their effectiveness under covariate shifts. Previous calibration methods under covariate shift struggle with class-wise or canonical calibrations and often rely on unstable importance weighting when density ratios are large or unbounded. Given the above limitations, this paper rethinks confidence calibration under covariate shifts. First, we derive a necessary and sufficient condition for confidence calibration under covariate shifts, named Expectation consistency condition, which reveals covariate shifts do not necessarily lead to uncalibrated confidence and provides a weaker condition for confidence calibration than global covariate distribution alignment. Then, utilizing Expectation consistency condition, this paper proposes an unsupervised domain adaptation loss to calibrate confidence of the target domain, named Expectation consistency loss (ECL), which is compatible with canonical calibration, class-wise calibration, and top-label calibration. Third, we prove that computing ECL loss has the same sample complexity as Expected Calibration Error (ECE) and provide a theoretically grounded mini-batch trainable scheme for ECL loss. Finally, we validate the effectiveness of our method on both simulated and real-world covariate shift datasets.

On MIMIC-IV, AUROC fell to 0.48-0.58, ECE rose to 0.68-0.76, and conformal coverage dropped from 0.80-0.98 to 0.21-0.25 against a 90% target. ### [15] [ConTact: Contact-First Antibody CDR Design via Explicit Interface Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21600)
*Mansoor Ahmed,Spencer VonBank,Nadeem Taj,Sujin Lee,Naila Jan,Murray Patterson*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有抗体CDR设计方法将"识别哪些CDR位置会接触抗原"和"在这些位置选择氨基酸"两个根本不同的子问题混为一谈，导致模型需通过统一消息传递隐式学习接触推理，抗原信号被均匀稀释到所有位置。

Method: ConTact采用接触-行动（contact-then-act）架构，包含三级级联：1) 学习表面互补指纹；2) 预测CDR-抗原接触；3) 将接触门控抗原特征注入序列头。其中距离偏置交叉注意力模块编码空间邻近先验，接触加权交叉熵损失将梯度信号集中在结合关键位置。

Abstract: Computational antibody CDR design methods condition on antigen structure to generate binding loops, yet existing architectures conflate two fundamentally distinct sub-problems: identifying which CDR positions will contact the antigen, and selecting amino acids at those positions. This conflation forces models to learn contact reasoning implicitly through uniform message passing, diluting antigen signal across all positions equally. We introduce ConTact, a contact-then-act architecture that explicitly decomposes CDR design into three cascaded stages: learning surface complementarity fingerprints, predicting CDR-antigen contacts, and injecting contact-gated antigen features into the sequence head. A distance-biased cross-attention module encodes geometric priors favoring spatial neighbors, while a contact-weighted cross-entropy loss concentrates gradient signal on binding-critical positions. On CHIMERA-Bench dataset, ConTact achieves the best structural quality (7% RMSD improvement over the next-best baseline), best epitope awareness (10% F1 score over GNN baselines), and competitive sequence recovery (AAR 0.38) among several CDR-H3 design baselines.

Conclusion: 推理蒸馏中教师令牌的可靠性是轨迹结构化的，可以通过位置权重有效利用，无需额外的教师计算。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) trains a student on its own rollouts using a privileged teacher, but its standard objective weights all generated tokens equally, implicitly treating the privileged teacher target as equally reliable at every student-visited prefix. Existing entropy-based OPD methods relax this uniformity by modulating token-level supervision with teacher entropy, but high teacher entropy in reasoning has an ambiguous reliability meaning: it can reflect either non-viable uncertainty or benign solution diversity. To identify this phenomenon, we introduce a branch-viability diagnostic. Specifically, we record next-token alternatives from the privileged-answer teacher prompt, force each alternative after the student prompt plus its on-policy spine prefix, and test whether the resulting student-template continuation recovers the correct answer. On Qwen3-4B, we find that an oriented within-sequence position score is the strongest tested predictor of teacher-token reliability, reaching an area-under-ROC-curve (AUROC) of 0.83; local uncertainty scores are at most 0.57. Motivated by this trajectory-level structure, we propose Position-Weighted On-Policy Self-Distillation (PW-OPSD), which applies an increasing position weight while keeping the same student rollout, privileged teacher pass, and clipped forward-KL target as OPSD. In our comprehensive evaluations with different random seeds, the diagnostic-derived PW-OPSD improves AIME 2024 and AIME 2025 Avg@12 by +1.0 and +1.1 points, and a generalization evaluation on two larger-scale models from different families, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B and Olmo-3-7B-Think, also demonstrates consistent aggregate Avg@12 improvements. These results show that teacher-token reliability in reasoning distillation is trajectory-structured and can be utilized without additional teacher computation.

</details>


### [17] [$\textit{BlockFormer}$ : Transformer-based inference from interaction maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21617)
*Eloïse Touron,Pedro L. C. Rodrigues,Julyan Arbel,Nelle Varoquaux,Michael Arbel*

Main category: cs.LG

Abstract: Inference from interaction maps, such as centromere identification from genome-wide chromosome conformation capture techniques -- notably Hi-C -- can be formulated as a generic inverse problem: infer a set of parameters given a map summarizing pairwise interactions between entities through blocks of variable numbers and sizes. In this work, we introduce a data-driven approach that leverages shared structure between these maps, such as global alignment between localized patterns, while handling the variability in number and size of entities arising in real-world data. Our approach relies on a transformer architecture capable of handling such variability and a custom simulator to generate abundant, yet computationally cheap synthetic data for training. Applied to the problem of centromere localization, the method accurately recovers their genomic positions across a wide range of species of various genome sizes.

### [18] [EntmaxKV: Support-Aware Decoding for Entmax Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21649)
*Gonçalo Duarte,Miguel Couceiro,Marcos V. Treviso*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EntmaxKV是一个面向entmax注意力机制的稀疏解码框架，通过利用entmax的稀疏性（产生精确零值），在KV页面加载前就实现稀疏化，在长上下文场景下相比全注意力基线可实现高达3.36倍（softmax）和5.43倍（entmax）的加速，同时保持接近全缓存entmax的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文解码中，KV缓存内存访问成为主要瓶颈，因为每个生成token都需要遍历随上下文长度线性增长的缓存。现有稀疏解码方法针对softmax注意力设计，但softmax的稠密尾部导致任何截断都会丢弃非零概率质量。而α-entmax产生精确零值，可将稀疏解码从稠密尾部近似转变为支持集恢复问题，但现有entmax核仅支持高效训练，未解决自回归解码中仍需要流式传输完整KV缓存的瓶颈问题。

Method: EntmaxKV包含三个核心组件：查询感知的页面评分（query-aware page scoring）、支持感知的候选选择（support-aware candidate selection）和稀疏entmax注意力。通过引入截断误差分析（基于丢弃概率质量δ），证明输出误差受δ控制且当entmax支持集被恢复时误差消失。还提出高斯感知的entmax选择器（Gaussian-aware entmax selector），从轻量级页面统计量估计entmax阈值，自适应调整所选预算以适应分数分布。

Result: 在匹配KV预算下，EntmaxKV相比基于softmax的稀疏解码方法丢弃更少的概率质量、保留更多的支持集token、实现更低的输出误差。在长上下文和语言建模基准测试上，EntmaxKV在使用一小部分KV缓存的情况下接近全缓存entmax的性能，在1M上下文长度下实现最高3.36倍（vs softmax全注意力）和5.43倍（vs entmax全注意力）的加速。

Conclusion: EntmaxKV通过利用entmax注意力固有的稀疏性，在KV页面加载前就实现稀疏化，有效解决了长上下文解码中KV缓存内存流量瓶颈问题，证明了entmax注意力在高效推理场景下的优势。

Abstract: Long-context decoding is increasingly limited by KV-cache memory traffic since each generated token attends over a cache whose size grows linearly with context length. Existing sparse decoding methods reduce this cost by selecting subsets of tokens or pages, but are designed for softmax attention, whose dense tails make any truncation discard nonzero probability mass. In contrast, $α$-entmax produces exact zeros, turning sparse decoding from dense-tail approximation into support recovery: if the selected candidates contain the entmax support, sparse decoding remains exact. While recent entmax kernels enable efficient training, they do not address the autoregressive decoding bottleneck, where dense inference still streams the full KV cache before sparsity is known. In this work, we introduce EntmaxKV, an entmax-native sparse decoding framework that exploits sparsity before KV pages are loaded. EntmaxKV combines query-aware page scoring, support-aware candidate selection, and sparse entmax attention. We analyze truncation error through the dropped probability mass $δ$, showing that output error is controlled by $δ$ and vanishes when the entmax support is recovered. We further introduce a Gaussian-aware entmax selector that estimates the entmax threshold from lightweight page statistics, adapting the selected budget to the score distribution. Empirically, EntmaxKV drops less probability mass, retains more support tokens, and achieves lower output error than softmax-based sparse decoding at matched KV budgets. On long-context and language modeling benchmarks, it closely matches full-cache entmax while using a small fraction of the KV cache, achieving up to $3.36\times$ (softmax) and $5.43\times$ (entmax) speedup over full attention baselines at 1M context length. Code available at: https://github.com/deep-spin/entmaxkv.

</details>

*Alexander Smirnov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AI文本检测器并非构建人机边界，而是放大预训练的典型性轴线；通过质心投影即可达到接近甚至超越微调的性能，该轴线在非母语写作中反转，且多种操作探针验证了观测者不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑现有AI文本检测方法的理论基础——检测器究竟是在学习区分人与AI文本的"边界"，还是仅仅放大了预训练阶段已存在的"典型性"轴线。

Result: 质心投影在RoBERTa-base上超越全微调；全微调反而降低对流畅正式文本的判别力；典型性轴线在非母语写作上完全反转（AUROC 0.06-0.20）；24样本冻结探针匹配全微调性能；闭式雅可比预测器实现R²=1.000的精确干预；三种操作探针高度一致（cos 0.74/0.81/1.00）；97%以上的LoRA→全微调偏差差距来自校准偏移而非表征学习。

Conclusion: AI文本检测的核心机制是放大预训练典型性轴线，而非构建人机分类边界；该发现具有跨架构、跨探测器的一致性和可迁移性，并对现有检测方法的解释和优化具有指导意义。

Abstract: AI text detectors amplify a pretrained typicality axis; they do not construct an AI-vs-human boundary. The same axis inverts on non-native ESL writing (AUROC 0.06-0.20) -- a falsifiable prediction unique to the typicality reading. A 24-example frozen probe matches full fine-tuning (0.900 vs 0.895). A closed-form Jacobian predictor parameterises axis-manipulating interventions with R^2 = 1.000 universal, lifts ELECTRA-CE deployment TPR from 0.000 to 0.904 at FPR = 1%, and transfers to three independently-trained third-party RoBERTa detectors at 16/16 oracle-equivalence (57% NYT-FPR reduction on the OpenAI detector). Scope: encoder family; mechanism magnitude HC3-anchored; population-level shared axis with per-text mechanisms varying across architectures. Three operationally distinct probes -- text-surface caps_rate residualisation, geometric signed-epsilon ablation, closed-form text-pair predictor -- agree at cos 0.74/0.81/1.00 across three architectures, confirming observer-invariance. Under matched-TPR-0.90 evaluation, the published intervention zoo (CC, dealign-f2c) is calibration-equivalent across 27 cells (|Delta AUROC| <= 0.0081), and >= 97% of the LoRA->full-FT bias gap on ELECTRA is calibration shift, not learned representation -- the central claim's prediction confirmed.

### [20] [Value-Gradient Hypothesis of RL for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21654)
*Arip Asadulaev,Daniil Ognev,Karim Salta,Martin Takac*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从值梯度视角解释了无批评者强化学习方法（如PPO、GRPO）在LLM后训练中的有效性，证明了在可微路径和加性噪声参数化下，actor更新在期望上等价于值梯度，并揭示了离散transformer策略中自动微分产生的经验代价态可近似值信号，最终提出了基于值梯度信号和可达奖励余量的RL效果分解准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无批评者强化学习方法（如PPO、GRPO）在预训练语言模型后训练中为何有效，以及它们在何种条件下能带来最大收益。

Method: 1) 在可微路径和加性噪声参数化下，证明actor更新的期望等价于值梯度；2) 对于离散transformer策略，证明通过注意力机制的自动微分产生的经验代价态可近似值信号，误差由采样间隔和策略熵控制；3) 将RL效果分解为值梯度信号和可达奖励余量。

Result: 无批评者RL的actor更新在期望上具有值梯度形式；自动微分可通过transformer注意力产生值信号近似；RL效果可分解为值梯度信号和可达奖励余量两部分。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了理解无批评者RL在LLM后训练中有效性的理论框架，并给出了判断RL沿预训练轨迹何时最有效的标准。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning substantially improves pretrained language models, but it remains understudied why critic-free methods such as PPO and GRPO work as well as they do, and when they should provide the largest gains. We develop a value-gradient perspective of critic-free RL for LLM post-training. First, under a differentiable rollout and additive-noise parameterization, we show that the actor update is value-gradient-like in expectation: the backward pass propagates costates whose conditional expectation equals the value gradient. Second, for discrete transformer policies, we show that autodifferentiation through attention produces empirical costates that approximate this value signal, with an error controlled by the sampling gap and policy entropy. These results motivate a decomposition of RL impact into value gradient signal and reachable reward headroom, yielding a criterion for when RL should be most effective along a pretraining trajectory.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型在下游任务（如逆问题）的适配中，通常需要昂贵的测试时引导或优化，计算成本高。本文旨在降低推理成本的同时生成高质量的奖励对齐样本。

Method: 将测试时适配形式化为层次变分模型，将控制摊销为轻量级但表达力强的随机策略；该策略支持大步长少步扩散采样，通过结构化每步控制维持样本质量；进一步扩展到半摊销机制，结合廉价摊销提议与有限测试时优化。

Abstract: Adapting pretrained diffusion models to downstream objectives such as inverse problems often requires expensive test-time guidance or optimization. We propose a principled framework for generating high-quality reward-aligned samples at substantially reduced inference cost. Our approach formulates test-time adaptation as a hierarchical variational model, where control is amortized into a lightweight yet expressive stochastic policy. This formulation naturally supports few-step diffusion sampling: large step sizes enable fast inference, while the learned policy maintains sample quality by providing structured per-step control. The resulting fully amortized sampler achieves a strong quality--speed tradeoff, matching or exceeding recent test-time scaling baselines while requiring significantly less compute. For example, on 4x super-resolution, our method achieves better perceptual quality with more than 5x faster inference compared to the best-performing baseline. We further extend our approach to a semi-amortized regime that combines cheap amortized proposals with limited test-time optimization, achieving state-of-the-art perceptual quality across several challenging inverse problems.

### [22] [I-SAFE: Wasserstein Coherence Metrics for Structural Auditing of Scientific AI Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21731)
*Barbara Tarantino,Gennaro Auricchio,Paolo Giudici*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出I-SAFE框架，一种基于Wasserstein相干性度量的后验分布审计方法，用于评估科学AI模型在结构引导扰动下的输出分布相干性，并在药物-靶标相互作用预测任务中展示了其超越传统精度评估的鉴别能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习模型在科学预测任务中常因利用捷径特征、数据集特定规律或分布偏差，导致强基准性能被错误解读为科学上有意义的行为，现有精度评估无法区分这些虚假关联。

Method: 提出I-SAFE框架，核心为Wasserstein相干性度量（WCM），包含三个互补指标：基于分位数的度量（QBM）评估位置级相干性、WCM评估序贯相干性、平移不变WCM变体评估形状相干性。对黑箱预测器施加结构引导的输入扰动，评估输出分布变化。

Result: 在Davis激酶基准、KLIFS结合口袋注释及三个序列DTI模型（DeepConvDTI、DeepDTA、TAPB）上，I-SAFE揭示了模型间显著不同的分布响应剖面，这种差异在精度评估中不可见。

Conclusion: I-SAFE是模型无关的审计框架，适用于任何输入可进行结构分解且存在外部先验知识的领域，能揭示传统精度评估无法捕获的模型行为差异。

Abstract: Deep learning models are increasingly used in scientific prediction tasks where strong benchmark performance is often interpreted as evidence of scientifically meaningful behavior. This interpretation is fragile, as models may exploit shortcut features, dataset-specific regularities, or distributional biases that are predictive on held-out data but not aligned with domain-relevant structure. To address this limitation, we introduce the \textsc{I-SAFE} (Interventional Secure, Accurate, Fair and Explainable) framework, a post-hoc distributional auditing framework for scientific AI models centered on the Wasserstein Coherence Metric (WCM). Given a trained black-box predictor and an external structural prior encoding domain knowledge about task-relevant input structure, \textsc{I-SAFE} evaluates raw model outputs under structurally guided perturbations of the input. The proposed audit measures output-distribution coherence through three complementary metrics: a Quantile-Based Metric (QBM) for location-level coherence, the WCM for ordinal coherence, and a translation-invariant WCM variant for shape coherence. We instantiate \textsc{I-SAFE} on drug--target interaction (DTI) prediction using the Davis kinase benchmark, KLIFS (Kinase--Ligand Interaction Fingerprints and Structures) binding-pocket annotations, and three sequence-based DTI models: DeepConvDTI, DeepDTA, and TAPB. Although the models operate in a comparable predictive regime, \textsc{I-SAFE} reveals substantially different distributional response profiles, a distinction invisible to accuracy-based evaluation. The framework is model-agnostic and applicable to any domain where inputs admit a structured decomposition and an external prior is available.

Abstract: Non-contrast computed tomography calcium scoring (CTCS) is widely recognized as an effective tool for cardiovascular risk stratification. This study aimed to develop a novel machine learning framework for predicting myocardial ischemia from routine non-contrast CTCS scans using quantitative coronary calcium assessment. This study analyzed 1,375 patients who underwent both non-contrast CTCS and regadenoson stress cardiac positron emission tomography myocardial perfusion imaging within one year at University Hospitals Cleveland Medical Center. Relevant features were identified using XGBoost with Shapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP). Predictive models were trained and evaluated using 5-fold cross-validation. Among 987 patients, 89 (9%) were positive for myocardial ischemia. The final model incorporated the Agatston score, eight calcium-omics features, and age. The proposed model achieved a precision of 98.9+/-3.0%, sensitivity of 79.2+/-8.4, and F1 score of 87.7+/-5.3%. The addition of calcium-omics features significantly improved predictive performance compared with models using clinical variables alone or clinical variables with the Agatston score (p<0.05). Interestingly, the number of calcified arteries, despite being the lowest-ranked feature based on SHAP analysis, showed the strongest association with myocardial ischemia in logistic regression analysis (odds ratio: 3.63, 95% confidence interval: 2.80-4.77, p<0.00001). We developed a machine learning approach for predicting myocardial ischemia using routinely acquired non-contrast CTCS scans. Calcium-omics features provided incremental predictive value beyond conventional risk factors and Agatston scoring and may support more accessible cardiovascular risk stratification.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文本到优化需要建模和绑定两种可分离的能力，现有模型在实例数据增长时精度急剧下降，存在有效绑定极限问题。

Method: 构建Text2Opt-Bench基准（12类优化问题），提出BIND推理方法将数值数据外化到结构化文件，使模型通过编程方式绑定数据而非从提示中转录。

Result: BIND在GPT-5-Nano上将准确率从59.1%提升至82.4%，GPT-5从86.2%提升至95.8%；1.5B绑定专用模型匹配7B端到端基线。

Conclusion: 绑定能力是制约文本到优化性能的关键瓶颈，可通过外化数据或专门化训练有效解决，且绑定能力可独立于建模能力进行分离式学习。

Abstract: Text-to-optimization requires two separable capabilities: modeling -- choosing the right optimization structure -- and binding -- grounding every coefficient, index, and parameter in the concrete problem data. We study this via Text2Opt-Bench, a scalable benchmark of solver-verified optimization problems spanning 12 categories, from textbook linear programs to stochastic and multi-objective formulations with up to thousands of variables. Across 10+ models, we find that accuracy collapses as instance data grows, even when the formulation itself is simple. We call this the effective binding limit. We address this via a simple inference-time approach, BIND, which externalizes numeric data to structured files so the model binds data programmatically rather than transcribing from the prompt. BIND improves GPT-5-Nano from 59.1% to 82.4% accuracy, matching pass@5 (82.0%) at lower token cost than pass@1, and GPT-5 from 86.2% to 95.8%. Furthermore, we validate our hypothesis by finetuning a model exclusively on binding and show that it outperforms end-to-end SFT and RL across three structurally distinct optimization categories, with a 1.5B binding specialist alone matching a 7B end-to-end baseline.

</details>


### [25] [PEARL: Unbiased Percentile Estimation via Contrastive Learning for Industrial-Scale Livestream Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21752)
*Blake Gella,Wei Wu,Yuhao Yin,Zexi Huang,Zikai Wang,Emily Liu,Junlin Zhang,Wentao Guo,Qinglei Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PEARL是一个非参数对比百分位近似框架，通过建模相对偏好信号而非绝对交互强度，有效缓解推荐系统中用户行为强度不平衡导致的偏差问题。离线实验和在线A/B测试（覆盖数十亿用户的直播平台）均验证其显著提升推荐性能。\n\n**亮点**：\n- 核心贡献：提出相对优势去偏方法，利用真实对比交互样本直接近似百分位关系\n- 理论保证：成对比较可无偏估计基于百分位的偏好信号\n- 技术增强：预测引导的自举平滑机制（稀疏/离散反馈）、广义值加权公式、协同训练策略\n- 在线收益：观看时长+2.10%，消费量+0.80%，互动率+1.49%，举报率-6.91%


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推荐系统存在用户行为强度不平衡问题——高活跃用户信号被过度放大，低活跃用户信号被低估，导致模型不能真实反映用户偏好，影响推荐质量和鲁棒性。

Method: 提出PEARL框架，核心方法包括：(1) 相对优势去偏，利用真实对比交互样本直接估计百分位关系；(2) 预测引导的自举机制处理稀疏/离散反馈的百分位平滑；(3) 广义值加权公式增强建模灵活性；(4) 协同训练策略提升表示学习。

Result: 离线实验有效缓解行为偏差，提升多排序目标的推荐性能；在线A/B测试在数十亿用户的直播平台中实现观看时长+2.10%、消费量+0.80%、互动率+1.49%、举报率-6.91%的显著改善。

Conclusion: PEARL通过建模相对偏好信号替代绝对交互强度，从理论上保证了无偏的百分位估计，在实际大规模推荐系统中取得了显著的性能提升，验证了该方法的有效性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Recommender systems trained on user interaction data are susceptible to behavioral intensity imbalance--a systematic distortion arising from heterogeneous engagement patterns across users. This imbalance skews feedback signals such that observed interactions no longer faithfully reflect true preferences, causing models to disproportionately amplify signals from highly active users while underrepresenting others, which ultimately degrades recommendation quality and robustness at scale. To address this issue, we propose a nonparametric contrastive percentile approximation framework, PEARL, that models relative preference signals instead of absolute engagement magnitudes. Building upon relative advantage debiasing, PEARL leverages real contrastive interaction samples to approximate percentile relationships directly, without relying on auxiliary distribution estimation models. We provide theoretical justification demonstrating that such pairwise comparisons yield unbiased estimates of percentile-based preference signals. For broader applicability, we introduce a prediction-based bootstrapping mechanism for percentile smoothing to handle sparse and discrete feedback, alongside a generalized value-weighted formulation and a co-training strategy to enhance both modeling flexibility and representation learning. Extensive offline experiments demonstrate that PEARL effectively mitigates behavioral bias and consistently improves recommendation performance across multiple ranking targets. Deployed in a production livestream platform with a combined user base of billions, online A/B testing confirms substantial real-world gains: +2.10% Watch Duration, +0.80% Consumption Amount, +1.49% Interaction Rate, and -6.91% Report Rate.

Abstract: We study risk-sensitive reinforcement learning in finite discounted MDPs, where a generative model of the MDP is assumed to be available. We consider a family or risk measures called the optimized certainty equivalent (OCE), which includes important risk measures such as entropic risk, CVaR, and mean-variance. Our focus is on the sample complexities of learning the optimal state-action value function (value learning) and an optimal policy (policy learning) under recursive OCE. We provide an exact characterization of utility functions $u$ for which the corresponding OCE defines an objective that is PAC-learnable. We analyze a simple model-based approach and derive PAC sample complexity bounds. We establish that whenever $u$ does not have full domain $\text{dom}(u)\neq \mathbb{R}$, the corresponding problem is not PAC-learnable. Finally, we establish corresponding lower bounds for both value and policy learning, demonstrating tightness in the size $SA$ of state-action space, and for a more restricted class of utilities, we derive lower bounds that makes the dependence on the effective horizon $\frac{1}{1-γ}$ explicit. Specifically, for $\text{CVaR}_τ$ we show that the correct dependence on $τ$ is $\frac{1}{τ^2}$, thus improving by a factor of $\frac{1}τ$ over state-of-the-art although our bound has a suboptimal dependence on $\frac{1}{1-γ}$.

### [28] [Memory-R2: Fair Credit Assignment for Long-Horizon Memory-Augmented LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21768)
*Sikuan Yan,Ahmed Bahloul,Ercong Nie,Susanna Schwarzmann,Riccardo Trivisonno,Volker Tresp,Yunpu Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Memory-R2训练框架，通过LoGo-GRPO算法（局部+全局组相对优化）解决多会话记忆增强型LLM智能体中因记忆状态不同导致轨迹级奖励不公平的问题，并联合优化记忆形成与演化，采用渐进式课程训练实现长程多会话学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多会话环境下用强化学习训练记忆增强型LLM智能体时，不同轨迹因写/更新/删除记忆导致中间记忆状态不同，破坏了GRPO等组相对方法要求"所有rollout来自相同有效环境"的假设，使得轨迹级奖励对长程记忆操作提供有偏的信用分配信号。

Method: 提出LoGo-GRPO算法：全局目标保持端到端长程轨迹级奖励学习；局部rerollout从相同中间记忆状态出发比较不同记忆操作结果，实现更公平的组比较和精确的记忆构建监督。采用共享参数协同学习设计，通过角色提示将同一LLM骨干实例化为事实提取器和记忆管理器，联合优化记忆形成与演化。采用渐进式课程训练（8→16→32会话）稳定长记忆跨度的多步RL。

Result: Memory-R2提供了在多会话长程场景下训练记忆增强型LLM智能体的有效范式，解决了记忆状态差异导致的信用分配不公平问题。

Conclusion: Memory-R2通过局部+全局组相对优化、共享参数协同学习和渐进式课程训练，为记忆增强型LLM智能体在长程多会话环境中的强化学习训练提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Memory-augmented LLM agents enable interactions that extend beyond finite context windows by storing, updating, and reusing information across sessions. However, training such agents with reinforcement learning in multi-session environments is challenging because memory turns the agent's past actions into part of its future environment. Once different rollouts write, update, or delete different memories, they no longer share the same intermediate memory state, making trajectory-level comparisons fundamentally unfair. This violates a key assumption behind group-relative methods such as GRPO, where rollouts are compared as if they were sampled from the same effective environment. Consequently, trajectory-level rewards provide noisy or biased credit signals for long-horizon memory operations. To address this challenge, we introduce Memory-R2, a training framework for long-horizon memory-augmented LLM agents. Its core algorithm, LoGo-GRPO, combines local and global group-relative optimization. The global objective preserves end-to-end learning from long-horizon trajectory-level rewards, while local rerollouts compare different memory-operation outcomes from the same intermediate memory state, yielding fairer group comparisons and more precise supervision for memory construction. Beyond credit assignment, Memory-R2 jointly optimizes memory formation and memory evolution with a shared-parameter co-learning design, where a fact extractor and a memory manager are instantiated from the same LLM backbone through role-specific prompts. To stabilize multi-step RL over long memory horizons, we adopt a progressive curriculum that increases the training horizon from 8 to 16 to 32 sessions. Together, these components provide an effective training paradigm for memory-augmented LLM agents in long-horizon multi-session settings.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将随机平滑与差分隐私的"隐私画像"（privacy profiles）概念建立联系，利用隐私画像提供的数值组合方法对异构机制（训练时和推理时的随机机制）进行组合分析，从而得到端到端的联合鲁棒性证书。具体以DP-SGD和Deep Partition Aggregation（推理时平滑）为例进行实例化。

Abstract: Randomized smoothing is a powerful tool for certifying robustness to adversarial perturbations, including poisoning attacks via randomized training and evasion attacks via randomized inference. Extending these guarantees to backdoor attacks, where training and test data are jointly perturbed, remains challenging because training- and test-time randomized mechanisms must be analyzed within a single robustness certificate. We address this by connecting randomized smoothing to the dual view of differential privacy through privacy profiles, which provide a numerical procedure for composing heterogeneous mechanisms. The resulting framework enables tight, modular, end-to-end certification of complex, composed mechanisms while leveraging existing analyses of differentially private mechanisms. We instantiate the framework for DP-SGD and Deep Partition Aggregation with inference-time smoothing, deriving joint robustness guarantees against both training-time and inference-time attacks. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework. Overall, we provide a principled and general framework for using composite mechanisms to certify robustness under complex threat models that better capture the capabilities of real-world adversaries.

### [30] [MMD-Balls as Credal Sets: A PAC-Bayesian Framework for Epistemic Uncertainty in Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21783)
*Ahanaf Hasan Ariq*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个PAC-Bayesian框架，通过最大均值差异（MMD）量化源分布与目标分布之间的偏移，并将MMD球解释为Walley不精确概率理论中的credal集，从而为测试时自适应（TTA）方法提供形式化的泛化保证和不确定性量化。论文建立了四个理论结果，并实现了认知不确定性与偶然不确定性的分离，以及自适应决策的准则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的TTA方法虽能提升分布偏移下的模型性能，但缺乏连接偏移大小与预测可靠性的形式化保证，即无法从理论上保证当分布偏移多大时模型输出仍可信。

Method: (i) 在RKHS-Lipschitz损失假设下，推导出含MMD依赖偏移惩罚项的PAC-Bayesian界；(ii) 通过MMD浓度不等式得到有限样本版本；(iii) 在credal集上推导均匀最坏情况风险界，并给出下-上风险分解；(iv) 建立测地线保持界，解释核引导自适应如何保护局部特征几何结构。

Result: 得到了四个理论结果：MMD参数化的PAC-Bayesian泛化界、有限样本界、均匀最坏情况风险界及其分解、测地线保持界。

Conclusion: 通过将MMD球解释为credal集，实现了认知不确定性与偶然不确定性的分离，并提供了何时进行自适应的原则性决策准则，从而为TTA方法提供了理论基础和可靠性保证。

Abstract: Test-time adaptation (TTA) methods improve model performance under distribution shift but lack formal guarantees connecting shift magnitude to prediction reliability. We develop a PAC-Bayesian framework yielding generalization bounds explicitly parameterized by the maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) between source and target distributions. Our principal contribution is interpreting MMD-balls around the source distribution as credal sets in Walley's imprecise probability theory, yielding natural epistemic uncertainty quantification. We establish: (i) a PAC-Bayesian bound with an MMD-dependent shift penalty under an RKHS-Lipschitz loss assumption; (ii) a finite-sample version via MMD concentration; (iii) a uniform worst-case risk bound over all distributions in the credal set, with a lower-upper risk decomposition; and (iv) geodesic preservation bounds explaining why kernel-guided adaptation protects local feature geometry. The credal set interpretation separates epistemic from aleatoric uncertainty and provides a principled decision criterion for when adaptation is warranted.

### [31] [Three Costs of Amortizing Gaussian Process Inference with Neural Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21798)
*Robin Young*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对一类潜在神经过程（LNP）与高斯过程（GP）之间的KL散度进行了理论界分析，将误差分解为标签污染、信息瓶颈和摊销误差三个可解释来源，并给出了误差随表示维度d的衰减速率，为神经过程的架构设计提供了理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经过程通过摊销学习将GP的$O(n^3)$后验推断近似为$O(n)$的映射，但这种摊销近似引入的误差缺乏严格理论刻画。本文旨在量化LNP与GP预测分布之间的差异，并解析误差来源。

Method: 利用KL散度将LNP与GP预测之间的差异分解为三项：标签污染（LNP用标签值估计GP中与标签无关的量）、信息瓶颈（有限维表示无法完整刻画上下文几何结构）和摊销误差（单一编码器跨上下文共享）。分别推导了瓶颈截断项在平方指数核（$O(e^{-cd^{2/d_x}})$）和Matérn-ν核（$O(d^{-2ν/d_x})$）下的衰减速率。

Result: 标签污染项在一般情况下为$O(1)$，仅观测噪声部分以$O(1/n)$衰减；瓶颈截断项的衰减速率直接关联核平滑度与输入维度；识别了通过标签相关表示路由不确定性估计的持久代价。

Conclusion: 给出了GP摊销机制下的架构建议：方差应仅从上下文位置预测，并用二阶池化替代均值聚合以缩小主要摊销差距。

Abstract: Neural processes amortize Gaussian process inference, replacing the exact $O(n^3)$ posterior with a learned $O(n)$ map from context sets to predictive distributions. For a class of latent neural processes, we bound the Kullback--Leibler (KL) divergence between the GP and LNP predictives, decomposing it into three interpretable sources, namely label contamination as the neural process uses label values to estimate a quantity that is label-independent in the exact GP, an information bottleneck because the finite-dimensional representation cannot resolve the full context geometry, and amortization error from a single encoder network shared across all contexts. The bottleneck truncation term decays in the representation dimension $d$ as $O(e^{-cd^{2/d_x}})$ for squared-exponential kernels on $\mathbb{R}^{d_x}$ where $c > 0$ is a kernel-dependent constant and as $O(d^{-2ν/d_x})$ for Matérn-$ν$ kernels, directly linking architecture sizing to kernel smoothness and input dimension. The label contamination term is $O(1)$ in general, with only the observation-noise component decaying as $O(1/n)$, identifying a persistent cost of routing uncertainty estimation through a label-dependent representation. These results characterize the costs of amortization within the analyzed class and yield architectural recommendations to predict variance from context locations alone in the GP-amortization regime, and replace mean aggregation with second-order pooling to close the dominant amortization gap.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有缩放定律将优化器视为固定的训练细节，忽略了优化器对表示缩放的影响。作者希望揭示优化器如何影响FFN表示的谱容量利用效率。

Result: AdamW在罕见token（TAIL）表示上硬谱秩缩放指数β=0.44（弱缩放），Muon达到β=1.02（线性缩放），提升2.3倍；优化器引起的谱偏移超过架构干预（注意力秩、位置编码）的影响；低损失不意味着表示结构相同。

Abstract: Scaling laws have made language-model performance predictable from model size, data, and compute, but they typically treat the optimizer as a fixed training detail. We show that this assumption misses a fundamental axis of representation scaling: how effectively the optimizer converts added FFN width into utilized spectral capacity. Using eigenspectra of feed-forward network representations, measured through soft and hard spectral-ranks, we find that \emph{the same Transformer architecture realizes markedly different spectral scaling laws when trained with different optimizers}. Holding architecture and width schedule fixed, AdamW exhibits weak hard-rank scaling ($β$=0.44) on rare-token (TAIL) representations where learning is known to be hardest, whereas Muon achieves linear scaling ($β$=1.02) in the same regimes, a $2.3\times$ increase in the scaling exponent. This difference is not reducible to validation loss: AdamW configurations can match low-rank Dion variants in perplexity, under extended training, while exhibiting sharply different spectral geometry, demonstrating that matched loss does not imply matched representation structure. Hard--soft rank asymmetry further reveals that optimizers differ not only in how much capacity is realized, but also in how that capacity is structured across eigenmodes. To disentangle optimizer effects from architectural ones, we compare against architectural interventions (e.g., attention rank and positional encoding), and find that optimizer-induced spectral shifts often exceed the architectural effects. These results suggest optimization as a first-class axis of representation scaling, motivating optimizer--architecture co-design.

### [38] [Energy-Gated Attention: Spectral Salience as an Inductive Bias for Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21842)
*Athanasios Zeris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出能量门控注意力（EGA），通过引入一个可学习的线性投影计算token嵌入的频谱能量，使得信息密集的token（如形态边界、句法核心、话语标记）获得更高注意力权重。在TinyShakespeare和Penn Treebank上，EGA仅增加0.26%参数便实现约0.1的验证损失改进，且无额外计算开销。实验表明固定小波基次优，最优的能量方向是数据自适应的非正弦方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Transformer注意力将所有token视为同等显著，忽略了token内在信息含量的差异。受湍流动力学中相干结构（携带大部分能量并主导输运）的启发，作者认为注意力中信息密集的token应类比相干结构，吸引更多注意力权重。

Method: 能量门控注意力（EGA）：通过一个可学习的线性投影计算key token嵌入的频谱能量，识别嵌入场的主频谱模式，然后依据该频谱能量对值聚合进行门控。仅增加一个线性投影层（约12,480参数），无额外计算成本。

Result: TinyShakespeare上验证损失提升0.103，Penn Treebank上提升0.101，参数量仅增加0.26%。学习到的能量阈值收敛到τ≈0.35，对应英语文本中约36%的token携带高于平均频谱能量，与英语实词比例一致。

Conclusion: 固定结构化小波基（Morlet、Daubechies等）是次优的，最优能量方向是数据自适应的非正弦方向；识别出学习小波包是一个有前景的开放方向。

Abstract: Standard transformer attention computes pairwise similarity between queries and keys, treating all tokens as equally salient regardless of their intrinsic informational content. In turbulent fluid dynamics, coherent structures -- the energetically dominant, spatially organized patterns that persist amid background chaos -- carry a disproportionate fraction of total energy and govern all transport. We propose that tokens play an analogous role in transformer attention: informationally dense positions (morphological boundaries, syntactic heads, discourse markers) concentrate spectral energy and should attract proportionally more attention than background tokens (function words, repeated patterns, low-information filler). We propose Energy-Gated Attention (EGA): a simple modification that gates value aggregation by the spectral energy of key token embeddings, computed by a single learned linear projection that discovers the dominant spectral mode of the embedding field. On TinyShakespeare, EGA achieves +0.103 validation loss improvement with only 12,480 additional parameters (<0.26% overhead) and no measurable computational cost. The result is consistent on Penn Treebank (+0.101), demonstrating dataset independence. A systematic ablation across three wavelet families (fixed Morlet, Daubechies db2/db4, and a parametric Morlet) establishes that fixed structured bases are suboptimal -- the optimal energy direction is data-adaptive and non-sinusoidal -- while identifying learned wavelet packets as a promising open direction. The learned energy threshold converges to tau ~= 0.35 independently of initialization, corresponding to the fraction (~36%) of tokens carrying above-average spectral energy in English text, a stable linguistic property consistent with the fraction of content words in running English text.

### [39] [Geometry-Adaptive Explainer for Faithful Dictionary-Based Interpretability under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21849)

Method: 提出了几何自适应解释器（GAE），通过将解释器字典与OOD活跃子空间重新对齐来缩小忠实度差距，同时保留原始特征结构。该方法仅需无标签的OOD激活值，无需梯度更新。理论上证明了GAE优于未适应的ID解释器，其额外损失受二阶矩偏移的二次界约束。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability aims to explain a model's behavior by identifying causally responsible internal structures. Dictionary-based explainers such as sparse autoencoders and transcoders are a primary tool, but their faithfulness under out-of-distribution (OOD) shift has received little systematic attention. We show that distribution shift rotates the subspace that the model actively uses, misaligning the explainer's dictionary trained on in-distribution (ID) activations. We formalize this misalignment as the faithfulness gap, a geometric distance between the ID dictionary and the OOD-active subspace, and show that it controls OOD faithfulness degradation. To reduce this gap, we propose the Geometry-Adaptive Explainer (GAE), which realigns the explainer's dictionary with the OOD-active subspace while preserving the original feature structure. This requires only unlabeled OOD activations and no gradient updates. We prove that GAE improves over the unadapted ID explainer, with excess loss bounded quadratically by the second-moment shift. Empirically, GAE even matches or surpasses all training-based baselines in causal faithfulness across multiple models and OOD settings.

TL;DR: 本文提出Zero-CoT Probe (ZCP)，一种通过截断思维链过程并对比同构扰动数据的黑盒检测方法，用于检测LLM中包括间接策略在内的数据污染，并引入Contamination Confidence指标量化污染程度。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据污染检测方法难以有效识别通过改写基准数据等间接（规避性）策略实施的隐蔽污染，且恶意模型发布者可能人为提升榜单表现，破坏了LLM推理能力评估的客观性。

Method: 发现模型生成的推理步骤会掩盖其记忆痕迹；提出ZCP方法，通过故意截断完整的思维链（CoT）过程以暴露潜在的捷径映射；进一步通过对比原始基准与同构扰动参考数据集上的零-CoT性能来分离记忆与内在解题能力；引入Contamination Confidence指标量化污染的可能性和严重程度。

Result: 在先前识别的污染模型和专门微调的污染模型上的大量实验表明，ZCP能够鲁棒地检测直接和间接的数据污染。

Conclusion: ZCP通过截断CoT暴露记忆痕迹，结合同构扰动对比和量化指标，有效检测了直接及规避性数据污染，为LLM评估的公正性提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive reasoning abilities across a wide range of tasks, but data contamination undermines the objective evaluation of these capabilities. This problem is further exacerbated by malicious model publishers who use evasive, or indirect, contamination strategies, such as paraphrasing benchmark data to evade existing detection methods and artificially boost leaderboard performance. Current approaches struggle to reliably detect such stealthy contamination. In this work, we uncover a critical phenomenon: a model's generated reasoning steps actively mask its underlying memorization. Inspired by this, we propose the Zero-CoT Probe (ZCP), a novel black-box detection method that deliberately truncates the entire Chain-of-Thought (CoT) process to expose latent shortcut mappings. To further isolate memorization from the model's intrinsic problem-solving capabilities, ZCP compares the model's zero-CoT performance on the original benchmark against an isomorphically perturbed reference dataset. Furthermore, we introduce Contamination Confidence, a metric that quantifies both the likelihood and severity of contamination, moving beyond simple binary classifications. Extensive experiments on both previously identified contaminated models and specially fine-tuned contaminated models demonstrate that ZCP robustly detects both direct and evasive data contamination. The code for ZCP is accessible at https://github.com/Yifan-Lan/zero-cot-probe.

</details>


### [41] [When to Switch, Not Just What: Transition Quality Prediction in Clash Royale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21868)
*Heeyun Heo,Huy Kang Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 通过对34,619名《皇室战争》玩家的92万余场对战记录分析，发现策略切换频率与胜率呈负相关。对此，论文提出TQP（Transition Quality Predictor）三阶段推荐管线（Who→When→What），通过PersonaGate、TimingGate和ScoreFusion三个模块实现个性化策略切换推荐，并引入无需最优行为假设的评估指标SwitchGap，在5.4%推荐率下取得+10.4个百分点的SwitchGap提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有策略推荐系统普遍基于“零切换成本假设”（Zero Switching Cost Assumption），即认为策略切换无行为代价且忽视个体切换倾向差异。然而实际游戏中，频繁切换策略的玩家胜率显著更低，这一矛盾揭示出传统方法忽略切换行为的隐形成本，亟需将策略推荐重构为过渡级别的决策问题。

Method: 提出TQP三阶段管线：（1）PersonaGate——抑制策略一致性经验上与更优结果相关的玩家的推荐；（2）TimingGate——通过亚类型和状态匹配的基线控制自然胜率恢复，识别切换净收益大于保持的时刻；（3）ScoreFusion——融合可采纳性信号与预测的过渡质量（Δ胜率）对候选策略排序。同时引入SwitchGap评估指标，不将观察到的玩家选择视为最优真实值。

Result: 完整管线在5.4%推荐率下实现+10.4个百分点的SwitchGap。损失触发的切换者（loss-triggered switchers）虽为最低表现群体，但从亚类型条件化指导中获益最多。

Conclusion: 策略切换存在显著的行为成本，个性化、时机敏感的推荐范式比传统基于期望质量的推荐更有效，尤其对表现最差的玩家群体改善最为显著。

Abstract: In competitive games, players frequently switch strategies after losing streaks, yet our analysis of 926,334 match records from 34,619 Clash Royale players reveals a counterintuitive pattern: switching frequency is inversely associated with the win rate, with effects that vary substantially across players and situational contexts. We attribute this to a limitation common in many prior recommendation systems, which evaluate strategies by expected quality while overlooking the behavioral cost of switching and individual differences in switching propensity. We refer to this implicit premise as the Zero Switching Cost Assumption. To address this, we reformulate strategy recommendation as a transition-level decision problem and instantiate it as TQP (Transition Quality Predictor), a three-stage pipeline structured as Who -> When -> What. PersonaGate suppresses recommendations for players whose strategic consistency is empirically associated with superior outcomes. TimingGate identifies moments when switching is likely to yield a net benefit over staying, using a subtype- and state-matched baseline to control for natural win-rate recovery. ScoreFusion ranks candidate strategies by combining an adoptability signal with predicted transition quality (delta WR). We further introduce SwitchGap, an evaluation metric that measures a policy's discriminative quality without treating observed player choices as optimal ground truth. This property is particularly important because the most frequent switchers record the lowest win rates. The full pipeline achieves a SwitchGap of +10.4 percentage points at a recommendation rate of 5.4%, and loss-triggered switchers, despite being the lowest-performing group, benefit the most from subtype-conditioned guidance.

</details>


### [42] [Noise Schedule Design for Diffusion Models: An Optimal Control Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21911)
*Seo Taek Kong,Weina Wang,R. Srikant*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于最优控制的框架来分析和设计扩散模型中的噪声调度，通过将问题转化为Fisher信息的ODE最优控制问题，证明了噪声调度与采样误差之间的理论联系，并推导出可实现最优采样误差的充分条件，同时提出了可泛化现有经验调度（如指数和Sigmoid调度）的闭式噪声调度表达式，通过参数调优在图像生成基准上取得了更优的FID分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型的理论工作虽然证明了$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$的最优采样误差界，但这些结果仅适用于特定的噪声调度，不包括实践中实际使用的调度（如指数调度、Sigmoid调度等）。因此，需要一个统一的原理性框架来分析和设计噪声调度，弥合理论与实践之间的差距。

Method: 将噪声调度设计问题重述为最优控制问题：状态为扩散过程的Fisher信息（遵循ODE演化），控制输入为噪声调度；目标函数为Fisher信息的泛函，该泛函被证明是KL散度采样误差的上界；通过求解该最优控制问题，推导噪声调度需满足的充分条件；进一步在数据分布参数化假设下，得到闭式噪声调度表达式，泛化指数调度和Sigmoid调度。

Result: 1) 获得了噪声调度需满足的充分条件，在该条件下$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$采样误差界可达；2) 在参数化假设下得到了可调参数的闭式噪声调度表达式，泛化了指数和Sigmoid调度；3) 系统调优这些参数在图像生成基准上取得了更优的FID分数。

Conclusion: 通过最优控制框架建立了噪声调度设计与采样误差之间的理论联系，既提供了理论保证（最优误差界），又产生了实践中可用的、性能优于标准经验调度的新噪声调度方案。

Abstract: We develop a principled framework for analyzing and designing noise schedules in diffusion models. We show that one can recast this design problem as an optimal control problem, whose state is the Fisher information of the diffusion process which evolves according to an ODE and the control input is the noise schedule. The objective of the optimal control problem is a functional involving the Fisher information, which is shown to be an upper bound on the Kullback-Leibler sampling error. By solving this optimal control problem, we obtain sufficient conditions on noise schedules under which state-of-the-art $\tilde{\mathcal{O}} (d/n)$ sampling error is achievable, where $d$ is the data dimension and $n$ is the number of discretization steps. While existing theoretical work also prove that $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$ sampling error bounds are achievable, these results hold for specific noise schedules, which do not include the schedules used in practice. Under a further parametric assumption on the data distribution, we show that one can obtain closed-form expressions for the noise schedules. These noise schedules generalize standard empirical schedules such as exponential and sigmoid schedules by allowing additional parameters that can be tuned. Systematically tuning the parameters of these schedules yields new schedules that achieve superior FID scores on image generation benchmarks.

### [43] [CausalGuard: Conformal Inference under Graph Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21928)
*Vikash Singh,Weicong Chen,Debargha Ganguly,Yanyan Zhang,Nengbo Wang,Sreehari Sankar,Mohsen Hariri,Alexander Nemecek,Chaoda Song,Shouren Wang,Biyao Zhang,Van Yang,Erman Ayday,Jing Ma,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CausalGuard 是一种结构加权共形框架，通过聚合图条件双重稳健伪结果和基于LLM先验的候选DAG加权校准，在观测数据中实现分布自由的有限样本边际覆盖，且条件均值收敛于真实CATE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观测数据中处理效应估计依赖于未知因果图的调整集选择，图误设会导致覆盖不足，而图无关的共形方法需大量填充才能恢复名义覆盖。

Method: 从LLM导出的边先验生成候选DAG，经条件独立性检验剪枝、BIC重新加权；聚合图条件双重稳健伪结果，构造复合非一致性分数进行后验加权校准。

Result: 在5个基准上，CausalGuard的平均覆盖率超过名义90%水平，且当图无关共形基线需要大填充时减少了宽度；压力测试表明其能抑制无效碰撞调整，在先验误设时仍保持稳定。

Conclusion: CausalGuard 提供了分布自由、有限样本保证的边际覆盖，在因果识别等条件下条件均值收敛于真实CATE，优于图无关共形方法。

Abstract: Estimating treatment effects from observational data requires choosing an adjustment set, but valid adjustment depends on an unknown causal graph. Graph misspecification can cause under-coverage, while graph-agnostic conformal wrappers may regain nominal coverage only through large padding. We introduce CausalGuard, a structure-weighted conformal framework that calibrates after aggregating graph-conditional doubly robust pseudo-outcomes. Candidate DAGs are proposed from an LLM-derived edge prior, pruned by conditional-independence tests, and reweighted by Bayesian Information Criterion. A composite nonconformity score then calibrates the posterior-weighted pseudo-outcome. CausalGuard provides distribution-free finite-sample marginal coverage for this aggregated pseudo-outcome; under causal identification, overlap, conditional-mean nuisance stability, and concentration on target-aligned valid adjustment strategies, its conditional mean converges to the true Conditional Average Treatment Effect. Across five benchmarks, CausalGuard attains mean coverage above the nominal 90% level for the directly evaluable target and reduces width when graph-agnostic conformal baselines require large padding. Stress tests show that CausalGuard suppresses invalid collider adjustment and remains stable under misspecified priors when the retained candidate set is data-supported.

### [44] [Optimal Guarantees for Auditing Rényi Differentially Private Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21938)
*Benjamin D. Kim,Lav R. Varshney,Daniel Alabi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于假设检验的审计框架，使用Donsker-Varadhan变分估计器直接估计Rényi散度；推导类受限DV估计量的非渐近置信区间；证明匹配的极小化最优下界。

Conclusion: 本文首次建立了基于DV估计器的RDP审计的最优样本复杂度保证，提出的审计框架在理论和实验上均优于现有黑盒审计方法。

Abstract: We study black-box auditing for machine learning algorithms that claim R \ 'enyi differential privacy (RDP) guarantees. We introduce an auditing framework, based on hypothesis testing, that directly estimates Rényi divergence between neighboring executions using the Donsker-Varadhan (DV) variational estimator. Our analysis yields explicit and non-asymptotic confidence intervals for RDP auditing via class-restricted DV estimators, separating statistical estimation error from algorithmic privacy leakage. We prove matching minimax lower bounds showing that, up to logarithmic factors, our sample-complexity guarantees are information-theoretically optimal, thereby establishing the first optimal guarantees for auditing RDP via DV estimators. Empirically, we instantiate our framework for auditing DP-SGD in a fully black-box setting. Across MNIST and CIFAR-10, and over a wide range of privacy regimes, our auditors produce a strong overall improvement on empirical RDP lower bounds compared to prior state-of-the-art black-box methods especially at small and moderate Rényi orders where accurate auditing is most challenging.

### [45] [SCI-Defense: Defending Manipulation Attacks from Generative Engine Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21948)
*Xucheng Yu,Haibo Jin,Huimin Zeng,Haohan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出SCI-Defense防御框架，结合困惑度检测、语义完整性评分和候选间检测，有效抵御针对LLM排序系统的生成式引擎优化攻击，在Amazon产品描述上达到Precision=1.000和FPR=0.000，同时揭示了现有防御手段的盲区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM排序系统易受GEO攻击，攻击者通过向产品描述注入语义信号来人为提升排名，现有防御手段对语义操纵攻击召回率为零，亟需有效的防御方案。

Method: 提出SCI-Defense三组件防御框架：1) 困惑度检测(PPL)；2) 语义完整性评分(SIS)，评估权威归因、叙事目的性、比较性声明和时间性声明四个操纵维度；3) 候选间检测(ICD)。

Result: 在600个Amazon产品描述上，SCI-Defense的Precision=1.000, FPR=0.000，对String、Reasoning和Review攻击的Recall分别为1.000、0.952和0.830。在MS MARCO上，String攻击被完美拦截，但对Review攻击召回率近乎为零，原因是网页段落缺乏说服导向信号。

Conclusion: 现有防御（PPL过滤、SafetyClf、释义）对语义操纵攻击完全无效；新发现的规范放大和用例饱和攻击暴露了语义相关性操纵这一结构性防御盲点，为未来研究指明了方向。

Abstract: LLM-based ranking systems are vulnerable to Generative Engine Optimization (GEO) attacks, where adversaries inject semantic signals into product descriptions to artificially boost rankings. We propose SCI-Defense, a three-component defense framework combining Perplexity detection (PPL), Semantic Integrity Scoring (SIS), and Inter-Candidate Detection (ICD). SIS evaluates four manipulation dimensions: Authority Attribution (AA), Narrative Purposiveness (NP), Comparative Claims (CA), and Temporal Claims (TC). Evaluated on 600 Amazon product descriptions across 6 categories, SCI-Defense achieves Precision=1.000 and FPR=0.000, with Recall of 1.000, 0.952, and 0.830 against String, Reasoning, and Review attacks respectively. On 600 MS MARCO web passages, String attacks are blocked with perfect recall while Review attacks yield near-zero recall, as web passages lack the persuasion-oriented signals that SIS targets in product descriptions. We demonstrate that existing defenses -- PPL-only filters, SafetyClf content classifiers, and paraphrasing -- achieve zero recall against semantic manipulation attacks. We further demonstrate new attacks such as Specification Amplification and Use-Case Saturation can expose semantic relevance manipulation as a structural defense blind spot that suggests directions for future research.

### [46] [Dynamic Mixture of Latent Memories for Self-Evolving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21951)
*Dianzhi Yu,Vireo Zhang,Hongru Wang,Yanyu Chen,Minda Hu,Wanghan Xu,Siki Chen,Philip Torr,Zhenfei Yin,Irwin King*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体自我进化方法要么通过更新模型参数导致灾难性遗忘，要么依赖外部记忆无法真正增强模型内在能力，亟需一种既能积累新知识又不会遗忘旧能力的持续学习框架。

Method: 基于动态混合专家（MoE）的生成式潜在记忆框架MoLEM：将多个专家作为独立记忆载体，通过路由器的键值匹配选择和加权专家，将聚合后的潜在记忆注入推理过程；基座模型完全冻结，经验知识内化到附加模块；每个训练阶段配对一个轻量级自编码器，推理时选择适当路由组，无匹配阶段则回退到预训练模型。

Result: 在数学、科学和代码领域的持续学习序列上，MoLEM相比原始预训练基线平均准确率提升10.40%，且没有其他竞争方法能在不同训练顺序下持续超越该基线。

Conclusion: MoLEM通过冻结基座模型并利用动态MoE内化经验知识，有效实现了持续学习中的知识积累与抗遗忘，显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Achieving self-evolution in intelligent agents requires the continual accumulation of new knowledge across changing task sequences without forgetting previously acquired abilities. Existing approaches either internalize knowledge by updating model parameters, which induces catastrophic forgetting, or rely on external memory, which fails to genuinely enhance the model's intrinsic capabilities. We propose MoLEM, a generative mixture of latent memory framework based on a dynamic mixture-of-experts (MoE). We treat multiple experts as independent carriers to generate memory. A router selects and weights experts through key-query matching, and the aggregated latent memory is injected into the reasoning process. The base model for reasoning remains entirely frozen, with all experiential knowledge internalized into the additional modules, avoiding catastrophic forgetting. For continual learning, each training stage is paired with a lightweight autoencoder that selects the appropriate routing group at inference, and inputs that match no stage fall back to the pretrained model. Experiments train the framework on continual-learning sequences spanning math, science, and code domains. After training, we evaluate the framework on the corresponding test sets to measure task learning and competence preservation across continual adaptation stages. After the full continual-learning sequence, our method improves the average accuracy by 10.40% over the Vanilla pretrained baseline, while none of the competing methods consistently exceed this baseline across different training orders.

### [47] [ChronoMedicalWorld: A Medical World Model for Learning Patient Trajectories from Longitudinal Care Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21963)
*Jiangyuan Wang,Xuyong Chen,Junwei He,Xu Xu,Shasha Xie,Fuman Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 ChronoMedicalWorld Model (CMWM)，一种面向长期临床轨迹预测的动作条件潜在世界模型，在慢性肾病 eGFR 预测任务上相比 GPT-5.5 结构化提示基线降低 MAE 7.28%、RMSE 7.35%，且框架不限于特定疾病。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: CMWM 包含联合嵌入状态编码器、宽动作编码器（支持结构化干预指标与自由文本沟通嵌入）、循环潜在转移模块，采用六项训练目标（下一步观测监督、下一步潜在预测、SIGReg 潜在正则化、三项生理学形状先验），并通过闭环 rollout-prefix 协议对齐训练与部署场景。

Result: 在 2,232 名 CKD 患者队列上，CMWM 的动态 50% 历史 rollout 测试 MAE 为 7.384、RMSE 为 10.256，优于 GPT-5.5 结构化提示基线的 7.964 和 11.069，改善主要来自医患对话部分。

Conclusion: CMWM 为慢性病长期轨迹预测提供了通用框架，其架构、损失设计和训练协议可迁移至任何可建模为周期性临床状态与结构化/对话式干预交替的慢性疾病。

Abstract: Long-horizon clinical simulation -- predicting how a patient's physiology evolves over years under specified interventions -- is central to chronic-disease care, yet existing electronic health record (EHR) models are predominantly discriminative, and general-purpose large language models drift under repeated interventions. We propose the \textbf{ChronoMedicalWorld Model (CMWM)}, an action-conditioned latent world-model framework for learning patient trajectories from longitudinal care data. CMWM couples a joint-embedding state encoder with a wide action encoder that admits both structured intervention indicators and free-text communication embeddings, and trains a recurrent latent transition module under a six-term objective: next-observation supervision, next-latent prediction, SIGReg latent regularisation, and three physiology-aware shape priors (slope, continuity, large-jump penalty). A closed-loop rollout-prefix protocol matches training to deployment, so the model is optimised against the same multi-step error it exhibits at inference. As a concrete case study, we instantiate CMWM for annual estimated glomerular filtration rate (eGFR) trajectory forecasting in chronic kidney disease (CKD). On a 2{,}232-patient nephrology cohort, the CKD instantiation achieves a dynamic-50\% history rollout test mean absolute error (MAE) of 7.384 and root-mean-square error (RMSE) of 10.256, against 7.964 and 11.069 for a tuned GPT-5.5 structured-prompting baseline ($-7.28\%$ MAE, $-7.35\%$ RMSE), with the gain dominated by the dialogue portion of patient--health-coach communication. The framework is not CKD-specific: its architecture, loss design, and training protocol apply to any chronic condition that can be cast as periodic clinical state interleaved with structured and conversational interventions.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文提出IAdaPID-ADG优化器，通过整合AMSGrad的非递增有效学习率和DiffGrad的梯度差调制因子，解决了AdaPID的收敛和稳定性问题，在多个数据集上显著优于现有优化器。
